The following table shows which ABAP language elements are allowed in which [ABAP language version](ABENABAP_VERSION_GLOSRY.html). While all language elements are allowed in [Standard ABAP](ABENSTANDARD_ABAP_GLOSRY.html), the set of usable elements is restricted in the [restricted ABAP language versions](ABENRESTRICTED_VERSION_GLOSRY.html)\\ [ABAP for Cloud Development](ABENABAP_FOR_CLOUD_DEV_GLOSRY.html) and [ABAP for Key Users](ABENABAP_FOR_KEY_USERS_GLOSRY.html).

**ABAP Language Element** **Standard ABAP** **ABAP for Cloud Development** **ABAP for Key Users**\\ [`_, IN range_tab`](ABENWHERE_LOGEXP_SELTAB.html) X X \\ [`_, LIKE`](ABENWHERE_LOGEXP_LIKE.html) X X writable_obj`](ABAPUPDATE_SET_EXPRESSION.html) X X \\ [`-=, Assignment Operator`](ABENCALCULATION_ASSIGNMENTS.html) X X \\ [`-=, REDUCE`](ABENCONSTRUCTOR_EXPRESSION_REDUCE.html) X X \\ [`->, Component Selector`](ABENOBJECT_COMPONENT_SELECTOR.html) X X \\ [`->*, Dereferencing Operator`](ABENDEREFERENCING_OPERATOR.html) X X \\ [`, , ABAP Language Element`](ABENCHAINED_STATEMENTS.html) X X \\ [`, , ABAP SQL Condition`](ABENWHERE_LOGEXP_IN.html) X X \\ [`, , SELECT - select_list`](ABAPSELECT_LIST.html) X X \\ [`, , SELECT GROUP BY`](ABAPGROUPBY_CLAUSE.html) X X \\ [`, , SELECT
